## Frequently asked questions

What is an integration?

An integration is a collection of pre-built dashboards and searches that give you added insight into the operation and/or security posture of a third-party solution.

Do the integrations cost anything?

No, they're free. For most third-party integrations you need to be an existing customer of both Sumo Logic and the outside solution. For two integrations, Security Analytics Integration & Integration for PCI Compliance, we do require professional services to get started.

Can I install multiple instances of the same integration?

Yes, we support multiple instances and environments. If you're looking to run a specific integration in dev, staging, and production we support that.

Do these integrations support logs as well as metrics?

Yes, all integrations support both logs and metrics.

What if I need to do a custom integration?

Sumo is built to be flexible and scalable. You're free to run your own queries and build custom dashboards to suit your needs. If you're looking for an integration we don't currently have an out-of-the-box solution for, we take requests in the ideas portal.

âSumo Logic has been instrumental for being able to monitor the overall playback experience, troubleshoot and resolve issues immediately to prevent any disruption to our services.â

## Frequently asked questions

What is an integration?

An integration is a collection of pre-built dashboards and searches that give you added insight into the operation and/or security posture of a third-party solution.

Do the integrations cost anything?

No, they're free. For most third-party integrations you need to be an existing customer of both Sumo Logic and the outside solution. For two integrations, Security Analytics Integration & Integration for PCI Compliance, we do require professional services to get started.

Can I install multiple instances of the same integration?

Yes, we support multiple instances and environments. If you're looking to run a specific integration in dev, staging, and production we support that.

Do these integrations support logs as well as metrics?

Yes, all integrations support both logs and metrics.

What if I need to do a custom integration?

Sumo is built to be flexible and scalable. You're free to run your own queries and build custom dashboards to suit your needs. If you're looking for an integration we don't currently have an out-of-the-box solution for, we take requests in the ideas portal.

âSumo Logic has been instrumental for being able to monitor the overall playback experience, troubleshoot and resolve issues immediately to prevent any disruption to our services.â

No, they're free. For most third-party integrations you need to be an existing customer of both Sumo Logic and the outside solution. For two integrations, Security Analytics Integration & Integration for PCI Compliance, we do require professional services to get started.

Can I install multiple instances of the same integration?

Yes, we support multiple instances and environments. If you're looking to run a specific integration in dev, staging, and production we support that.

Do these integrations support logs as well as metrics?

Yes, all integrations support both logs and metrics.

What if I need to do a custom integration?

Sumo is built to be flexible and scalable. You're free to run your own queries and build custom dashboards to suit your needs. If you're looking for an integration we don't currently have an out-of-the-box solution for, we take requests in the ideas portal.

âSumo Logic has been instrumental for being able to monitor the overall playback experience, troubleshoot and resolve issues immediately to prevent any disruption to our services.â

## Your Choices Regarding Cookies on this Site

We use cookies and similar tracking technologies, and we allow our advertising partners to use such technologies, so we can, among other things, show you ads promoting Sumo Logic on other sites and services. These activities may be considered âsales,â âsharing,â or âtargeted advertisingâ under certain privacy laws, and you may have the right to opt out.
To opt-out of these activities, uncheck "All cookies" below. Note that you will need to renew this opt-out choice if you visit our website from another device or browser or if you clear your cookies. You can also opt out by visiting our website with a legally-recognized opt-out preference signal, such as the Global Privacy Control.

Allow All

### Manage Consent Preferences

#### Strictly Necessary Cookies

Always Active

These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

#### All cookies

All cookies

- ##### Performance Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.


- ##### Functional Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.


- ##### Targeting Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.

## Frequently asked questions

What is an integration?

An integration is a collection of pre-built dashboards and searches that give you added insight into the operation and/or security posture of a third-party solution.

Do the integrations cost anything?

No, they're free. For most third-party integrations you need to be an existing customer of both Sumo Logic and the outside solution. For two integrations, Security Analytics Integration & Integration for PCI Compliance, we do require professional services to get started.

Can I install multiple instances of the same integration?

Yes, we support multiple instances and environments. If you're looking to run a specific integration in dev, staging, and production we support that.

Do these integrations support logs as well as metrics?

Yes, all integrations support both logs and metrics.

What if I need to do a custom integration?

Sumo is built to be flexible and scalable. You're free to run your own queries and build custom dashboards to suit your needs. If you're looking for an integration we don't currently have an out-of-the-box solution for, we take requests in the ideas portal.

âSumo Logic has been instrumental for being able to monitor the overall playback experience, troubleshoot and resolve issues immediately to prevent any disruption to our services.â

These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.


- ##### Targeting Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.

## Frequently asked questions

What is an integration?

An integration is a collection of pre-built dashboards and searches that give you added insight into the operation and/or security posture of a third-party solution.

Do the integrations cost anything?

No, they're free. For most third-party integrations you need to be an existing customer of both Sumo Logic and the outside solution. For two integrations, Security Analytics Integration & Integration for PCI Compliance, we do require professional services to get started.

Can I install multiple instances of the same integration?

Yes, we support multiple instances and environments. If you're looking to run a specific integration in dev, staging, and production we support that.

Do these integrations support logs as well as metrics?

Yes, all integrations support both logs and metrics.

What if I need to do a custom integration?

Sumo is built to be flexible and scalable. You're free to run your own queries and build custom dashboards to suit your needs. If you're looking for an integration we don't currently have an out-of-the-box solution for, we take requests in the ideas portal.

âSumo Logic has been instrumental for being able to monitor the overall playback experience, troubleshoot and resolve issues immediately to prevent any disruption to our services.â

## Your Choices Regarding Cookies on this Site

We use cookies and similar tracking technologies, and we allow our advertising partners to use such technologies, so we can, among other things, show you ads promoting Sumo Logic on other sites and services. These activities may be considered âsales,â âsharing,â or âtargeted advertisingâ under certain privacy laws, and you may have the right to opt out.
To opt-out of these activities, uncheck "All cookies" below. Note that you will need to renew this opt-out choice if you visit our website from another device or browser or if you clear your cookies. You can also opt out by visiting our website with a legally-recognized opt-out preference signal, such as the Global Privacy Control.

Allow All

### Manage Consent Preferences

#### Strictly Necessary Cookies

Always Active

These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

#### All cookies

All cookies

- ##### Performance Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.


- ##### Functional Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.


- ##### Targeting Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.

### About Sumo Logic

Sumo Logic Inc., (NSDQ: SUMO) is the pioneer in continuous intelligence, a new category of software, which enables organizations of all sizes to address the data challenges and opportunities presented by digital transformation, modern applications, and cloud computing. The Sumo Logic Continuous Intelligence Platformâ¢ automates the collection, ingestion, and analysis of application, infrastructure, security, and IoT data to derive actionable insights within seconds. More than 2,100 customers around the world rely on Sumo Logic to build, run, and secure their modern applications and cloud infrastructures. Only Sumo Logic delivers its platform as a true, multi-tenant SaaS architecture, across multiple use-cases, enabling businesses to thrive in the Intelligence Economy. For more information, visit [www.sumologic.com.](http://www.google.com/url?q=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.sumologic.com%2F&sa=D&sntz=1&usg=AFQjCNEkzBKVzZU1fc2SBDpK9XbSbZnVDg)

_Sumo Logic_ is a trademark or registered trademark of Sumo Logic in the United States and in foreign countries. All other company and product names may be trademarks or registered trademarks of their respective owners.

Any information regarding offerings, updates, functionality, or other modifications, including release dates, is subject to change without notice. The development, release, and timing of any offering, update, functionality, or modification described herein remains at the sole discretion of Sumo Logic, and should not be relied upon in making a purchase decision, nor as a representation, warranty, or commitment to deliver specific offerings, updates, functionalities, or modifications in the future.

## Your Choices Regarding Cookies on this Site

We use cookies and similar tracking technologies, and we allow our advertising partners to use such technologies, so we can, among other things, show you ads promoting Sumo Logic on other sites and services. These activities may be considered âsales,â âsharing,â or âtargeted advertisingâ under certain privacy laws, and you may have the right to opt out.
To opt-out of these activities, uncheck "All cookies" below. Note that you will need to renew this opt-out choice if you visit our website from another device or browser or if you clear your cookies. You can also opt out by visiting our website with a legally-recognized opt-out preference signal, such as the Global Privacy Control.

Allow All

### Manage Consent Preferences

#### Strictly Necessary Cookies

Always Active

These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

#### All cookies

All cookies

- ##### Performance Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.


- ##### Functional Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.


- ##### Targeting Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.

## Video Guidelines and Assets
[iframe](https://117583536.intellimizeio.com/storage.html)Video guidelines and assets \| Sumo Logic [\\_\\_\\_](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/video-assets/#)

# Video guidelines and assets

## Sumo Logic Brand

- [Sumo Logic Brand Guidelines](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/introduction/)
- [Who we are](https://www.sumologic.com/company/about-us/)
- [Boilerplate](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/boilerplate/)
- [Logo](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/logo/)
- [Symbol lockup](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/symbol-lockup/)
- [Video guidelines & assets](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/video-assets/)
- [Press kit](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/press-kit/)

In order to reinforce our branding, it is crucial that all video content be exported at the appropriate settings and format. The end-board animation must be used in all published videos.

All storyboard and draft edit of each video needs to be reviewed by the brand team. Please submit storyboard or videos to [ask-brand@sumologic.com](mailto:ask-brand@sumologic.com)

## [Copy heading link](https://sites.google.com/sumologic.com/sumo-logic-brand-external/video-guidelines-assets\#h.zfq2n3pvcy8s) Aspect ratio

All videos should be recorded in a 16:9 widescreen aspect ratio with at least 29.97 FPS in high-definition. The recommended video size is 1920x1080.

## [Copy heading link](https://sites.google.com/sumologic.com/sumo-logic-brand-external/video-guidelines-assets\#h.iwu5shpwchx1) Copy & Typeface

All videos should use our primary typeface, [Lab Grotesque](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/resources/brand/SumoLogicFont-LabGrotesqueCompleteOT.zip).

All copy should be in sentence case formatting. The one exception is: proper nouns, which are always title case (initial cap).

## Lower third

If we are introducing someone in the video, a lower third graphic may be used to introduce the person's name, company, and their title.

To use this lower third template, edit the proper name/title in Photoshop. Once that is completed, save the PSD file and import the layers into your video editor.

**Transition effects**

Fade-in time: 00:00:02:00 (2 seconds)

Static frame: ~ 00:00:07:00 (Around 5 seconds)

Fade-out time: 00:00:02:00 (2 seconds)

[Download lower third PSD template](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/resources/brand/SumoLogic-Lower-Third-Template.zip)

![Lower third](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/landing-pages/sumo-logic-lower-third.png)

## **Dialogue &** **n** **arration**

It is pertinent to speak clearly and slowly when recording any dialogue or narration for videos. Your tone and energy can dictate the mood of your audience. When possible, please isolate your voice or narration from any background noise that might be distracting. An external microphone is highly recommended for recording. Try to do all recordings with the same equipment and room/environment for a consistent sound.

**All dialogue or narration should come to a stop before the end-board animation sequence.**

## [Copy heading link](https://sites.google.com/sumologic.com/sumo-logic-brand-external/video-guidelines-assets\#h.uxlj2hkekbaf)**Music &** **s** **oundtrack**

Currently there is no official "sound" or "music" for Sumo Logic. When using music for your videos, please ensure we have full rights and license specifically for commercial-use. Music may play through the end-board animation and fade-out by the last frame for a seamless experience.

Please use good judgement on what music is appropriate for your video. Make sure the volume is not too loud and drowns out any dialogue if present. When in doubt, please contact the Brand Team for guidance.

## Sumo Logic watermark

The Sumo Logic watermark maximizes our brand presence in videos. Please use the following watermark template when creating your video. The watermark sits directly at the bottom-right edge of the title safe guideline and just inside the action safe line.

To use the watermark template, simply place this PSD layer on top of your video content.

**Make sure the Sumo Logic watermark does not appear over our endboard animation.**

[Download 16:9 watermark template](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/resources/brand/SumoLogic-watermark-16-9-template-final.zip)

![Sumo Logic watermark](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/landing-pages/sumo-logic-watermark-positioning.png)

## End-board animation

Add one of these animation clip to your video timeline so the end-board plays after your video content. This is for external and internal videos and videos associated with Sumo Logic events. There are 2 sound options and a silent version available for use. See guidelines below to ensure which end board animation to use for your video.

**All dialogue or narration in video must come to a stop before any of the end-board animations.**

### My video has music

â Use the silent endboard animation

â Must have the music in your video play through to the end of the end-board animation

### My video does not have any music

â Use any end-board anmation with sound or no sound

### Corporate end-board

The "See business differently with continuous intelligence" end-board animation may be used as a primary brand and corporate logo sign off in applications where both logo and tagline is needed.

![](https://assets-testing.sumologic.com/logos/app/Corporate-end-board.png)

[Download corporate tagline lockup end-board animation](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/resources/brand/SumoLogic-Endtag-Animation-CIP.zip)

### Product and solution tagline lockup end-board

The "Continuous Intelligence Platformâ¢" end-board animation may be used as a logo sign off for the Continuous Intelligence Platform, product solutions or offerings where both logo and tagline is needed.

![](https://assets-testing.sumologic.com/logos/app/Product-and-solution-tagline-lockup-end-board.png)

[Download product and solution tagline lockup animation](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/resources/brand/SumoLogic-Endtag-Animation-SBD-CIP.zip)

## Export settings

**H.264** \- This is the preferred method of video encoding that will maximize quality with low bitrate and file size. Upon export, the H.264 compression will create a .MP4 video file. When possible, this is the setting you should use for optimal upload speed and playback for YouTube or Vimeo. If your video uses alpha channels or transparencies, do not use this.

**.MOV** \- Quicktime's .mov is the preferable choice for exporting videos with an Alpha Channel.

**.AVI** \- While this produces the best quality image, the file size is generally very large and can create a lag during playback if the .AVI file is uncompressed. AVIs can support videos with Alpha Channel.

## Sumo Logic Symbol Lockup
[iframe](https://117583536.intellimizeio.com/storage.html)Symbol lockup \| Sumo Logic

# Symbol lockup

## Sumo Logic Brand

- [Sumo Logic Brand Guidelines](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/introduction/)
- [Who we are](https://www.sumologic.com/company/about-us/)
- [Boilerplate](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/boilerplate/)
- [Logo](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/logo/)
- [Symbol lockup](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/symbol-lockup/)
- [Video guidelines & assets](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/video-assets/)
- [Press kit](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/press-kit/)

## Symbol lockup

The symbol lockup can be used in cases where a singular application of both [logo](https://sites.google.com/sumologic.com/sumo-logic-brand-external/logo) and [symbol](https://sites.google.com/sumologic.com/sumo-logic-brand-external/symbol) is needed.

**Please note: The SUMO in the square is a color - either white or Sumo blue. It is never a cutout, and it is never black or any other color. See examples below for the correct color application based on type of background. The only exception if it's being printed on glass or a material where the SUMO absolutely cannot be white or Sumo blue.**

![Symbol lockup](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/landing-pages/sumo-logic-symbol-lockup.jpg)

## **Symbol lockup color**

**Color symbol lockup options**

There are two color symbol lockups; one that should only be used on a light background, and the other that should only be used on a dark background.

**Black symbol lockup**

Use the black symbol lockup when reproduction is limited to black and white or if your overall color palette is monochromatic. It is to be used only against light backgrounds.

**Reversed symbol lockup**

Use the reverse symbol lockup on dark backgrounds only.

![Color symbol lockup on a light background](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/icons/Color-symbol-lockup-on-a-light-background.jpg)

Color symbol lockup on a light background

_Note: SUMO in a colored square is always white; it is NEVER a cut out_

![Color symbol lockup on a dark background](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/icons/Color-symbol-lockup-on-a-dark-background.jpg)

Color symbol lockup on a dark background

_Note: SUMO in a colored square is always white; it is NEVER a cut out_

![Black symbol lockup on a light background](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/icons/Black-symbol-lockup-on-a-light-background.jpg)

Black symbol lockup on a light background

_Note: SUMO in a colored square is always white; it is NEVER a cut out_

![Reversed White symbol lockup on a dark background](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/icons/Reversed-White-symbol-lockup-on-a-dark-background.jpg)

Reversed/White symbol lockup on a dark background

_Note: SUMO in a white square is always Sumo blue; it is NEVER a cut out_

## Clear space

Follow the specifications below for the required amount of clear space to ensure maximum visibility and legibility. The clear space is defined by .5x the height of the square.

![Clear space](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/landing-pages/sumo-logic-symbol-lockup-height.jpg)

## Minimum size

Follow the specifications below for the required minimum size to ensure maximum visibility and legibility.

![Minimum size](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/landing-pages/Minimum-size.png)

## Usage

The symbol lockup is not Sumo Logicâs logo. It can be used when the presence of the symbol is necessary but the logo is required due to legality. Only used symbol lockup assets provided. Do not create new versions of the lockup.

![Usage](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/landing-pages/sumo-logic-symbol-usage.png)

## Placement

The location of the symbol lockup in layouts is important for recognition, especially when seen multiple times across various touch points. In most cases, the location is media driven and the main consideration becomes visibility of the Sumo Logic symbol lockup over a consistent location.

![Placement](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/landing-pages/sumo-logic-symbol-placement.png)

## Alignment

When placing the symbol lockup consider the alignment with the grid, type, and graphic or image. The symbol lockup is primarily centered on applications.

![Alignment](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/landing-pages/sumo-logic-symbol-alignment.png)

[Download symbol lockup](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/resources/brand/SumoLogic-Symbol-Lockup.zip)

## Sumo Logic Logo Guidelines
[iframe](https://117583536.intellimizeio.com/storage.html)Logo \| Sumo Logic [\\_\\_\\_](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/logo/#)

# Logo

## Sumo Logic Brand

- [Sumo Logic Brand Guidelines](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/introduction/)
- [Who we are](https://www.sumologic.com/company/about-us/)
- [Boilerplate](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/boilerplate/)
- [Logo](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/logo/)
- [Symbol lockup](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/symbol-lockup/)
- [Video guidelines & assets](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/video-assets/)
- [Press kit](https://www.sumologic.com/brand-guidelines/press-kit/)

The Sumo Logic logo is the most concise and visible representation of our brand. The logo is made up of a customized wordmark and may not be altered in any way. In logo format, Sumo Logic is represented in all lower case. In written format, Sumo Logic should always appear as two words in title case. In order to develop a consistent experience and perception of Sumo Logic, complete adherence to these logo usage guidelines across all applications should be the mandate.

![Sumo Logic Brand Guidelines Logo](https://assets-testing.sumologic.com/logos/app/sumologic-bg-logo.png)

## [Copy heading link](https://sites.google.com/sumologic.com/sumo-logic-brand-external/logo\#h.p_9UgDas5p_I4d) Color versions

**Color and reversed logo**

There are two primary versions of the Sumo Logic logo: color and reversed. Always use the color version against a white background. It may also be applied over light background colors when white is not available.

The reversed logo works best when reversed out of the primary Sumo Logic blue as well as darker colors that provide enough contrast. (see color section)

**Black logo**

Use the black version of the Sumo Logic word mark when reproduction is limited to black and white or if your overall color palette is monochromatic.

**Please note: The Sumo Logic logo is either white, black or Sumo blue. See examples below for the correct color application based on type of background.**

**The only exception if it's being printed on glass or a material where the** **logo** **absolutely cannot be white, black or Sumo blue.**

![Color logo](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/application-content/color-logo.png)

### Color logo

![Reversed logo](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/application-content/reversed-logo.png)

### Reversed logo

![Black logo](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/application-content/black-logo.png)

### Black logo

## Clear space

Clear space, minimum size, registered trademark

**Clearspace and minimum size**

Follow the specifications below for the required amount of clear space and minimum size to ensure maximum visibility and legibility. The clear space is defined by the height of the âlâ in sumo logic.

![Clear space](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/landing-pages/clear-space.png)

## Registered trademark

In most cases, the registered trademark symbol is not included with the logo because it is most commonly used in digital environments. There are several circumstances\* that may require the addition of the Â®.

\*You may opt to use the wordmark with registration symbol in formal applications such as legal documents and / or business systems where the registration symbol notates trademark status.

![Registered trademark](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/landing-pages/registered-trademark.png)

![Do not change or add colors](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/application-content/Do-not-change-or-add-colors.png)

### Do not change or add colors

### Do not lock up copy to logo

## **Usage examples**

![](https://assets-testing.sumologic.com/logos/app/Usage-examples.png)

## **File formats**

Sumo Logic logos are provided in three color versions and several file formats. All files have been created at sizes common to their media, and should not be altered, recolored, scaled disproportionately, or modified in any way. The chart below details the file formats best suited for each use case.

For print applications, CMYK (Cyan, Magenta, Yellow, Black) and PMS (Pantone Matching System) assets are available in AI and EPS format. For on-screen use, RGB assets come in two file formats. SVG files are vector based, and can be scaled to any size. PNG files have transparent backgrounds and a fixed resolution, which can be scaled down (but not up) in size.

![](https://assets-testing.sumologic.com/logos/app/File-formats.png)

## Your Choices Regarding Cookies on this Site

We use cookies and similar tracking technologies, and we allow our advertising partners to use such technologies, so we can, among other things, show you ads promoting Sumo Logic on other sites and services. These activities may be considered âsales,â âsharing,â or âtargeted advertisingâ under certain privacy laws, and you may have the right to opt out.
To opt-out of these activities, uncheck "All cookies" below. Note that you will need to renew this opt-out choice if you visit our website from another device or browser or if you clear your cookies. You can also opt out by visiting our website with a legally-recognized opt-out preference signal, such as the Global Privacy Control.

Allow All

### Manage Consent Preferences

#### Strictly Necessary Cookies

Always Active

These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

#### All cookies

All cookies

- ##### Performance Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.


- ##### Functional Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.


- ##### Targeting Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.

# Sumo Logic brand guidelines

## Sumo Logic Brand

## **Welcome!**

The goal of this site is to establish the brand system of Sumo Logic - its story, visual identity, voice and brand language -- to drive a consistent brand presence across all target audiences: employees, customers, partners, prospects, candidates, investors and industry influencers. Thanks to all of you for supporting the Sumo Logic Brand, and for your enthusiasm for being a Sumo brand ambassador!

## [Copy heading link](https://sites.google.com/sumologic.com/sumo-logic-brand-external/sumo-logic-brand-guidelines\#h.sl2dlehexvlm)**Brand review and questions**

We expect our brand system to grow over time as we add more graphical elements, assets, and applications. Therefore, all brand designs created using our brand system will need a review by our Sumo Logic brand team to ensure consistency and compliance. We will strive to deliver a 24-hour-or-less turnaround. Share your asset with us or writing style questions at [ask-brand@sumologic.com](mailto:ask-brand@sumologic.com).

#### Flexible licensing

### Leave Relics behind..

[Explore the platformâ](https://www.sumologic.com/compare/sumo-logic-vs-new-relic/)

#### Unlimited users

| Cloud architecture<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>QRadar is a lift-and-shift version of its on-prem solution, requiring additional provisioning at additional cost for ingesting and searching at scale<br>Sumo Logic is Cloud Native multi-tenant platform that can instantly scale each component of the architecture up or down to meet customer demand. |  |  |
| Breadth of portfolio<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>While QRadar has a comprehensive portfolio (logs, EDR, SIEM, and SOAR) but itâs very complex and costly to implement, often requiring professional services<br>Sumo Logic offers a unified platform for observability (logs metrics, APM/Traces, and RUM) and security (security data lake, audit, and compliance, Cloud SIEM and Cloud SOAR), assisting with tool consolidation. |  |  |
| Collect<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>QRadar on Cloud requires the installation of a data gateway appliance, which is used to connect to the instance of QRadar running in the IBM cloud.<br>Sumo Logic is a platform/vendor agnostic with the ability to collect logs and security-relevant data across your on-prem, cloud and multi-cloud environments without the need for additional hardware |  |  |
| Threat Intel Platform<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>QRadar offers Integrated TIP however requires the purchasing of IBM Advanced Threat Protection Feed at an additional cost<br>Sumo Logic includes an integrated, out-of-the-box TIP, leveraging CrowdStrike (OEM) to help add threat dimensions to the security events. | Fixed data structure<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>In QRadar, everything needs to be pre-parsed to facet the fields for you to look for something. If a certain field has not already been parsed, youâre stuck doing keyword searches.<br>Sumo Logic fully indexes all log data â structured and unstructured â without having data adhere to indexes with defined schemas allowing for quick time to value and flexibility. |  |  |
| Licensing<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>QRadar licenses based on the number of employees (1 EPS per employee) with 30-day retention.<br>Sumo Logic offers a simple credit-based licensing model that offers predictability and flexibility and enables frictionless expansion to align with use cases without charging based on users. |  |  |

## Your Choices Regarding Cookies on this Site

We use cookies and similar tracking technologies, and we allow our advertising partners to use such technologies, so we can, among other things, show you ads promoting Sumo Logic on other sites and services. These activities may be considered âsales,â âsharing,â or âtargeted advertisingâ under certain privacy laws, and you may have the right to opt out.
To opt-out of these activities, uncheck "All cookies" below. Note that you will need to renew this opt-out choice if you visit our website from another device or browser or if you clear your cookies. You can also opt out by visiting our website with a legally-recognized opt-out preference signal, such as the Global Privacy Control.

Allow All

### Manage Consent Preferences

#### Strictly Necessary Cookies

Always Active

These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

#### All cookies

All cookies

- ##### Performance Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.


- ##### Functional Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.


- ##### Targeting Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.

## Why is Sumo Logic a better alternative than New Relic?

The more complex application architectures get, the more teams need to work together to deliver reliable and secure apps. Give **all** your users easy access to unified security and observability. Monitor, troubleshoot and secure your apps and infrastructure from a single SaaS analytics platform.

Don't let expensive per-seat licensing hold your real-time insights hostage!

| [Expand all](https://www.sumologic.com/compare/sumo-logic-vs-new-relic/#) | ![Sumo Logic](https://www.sumologic.com/img/logo-black.svg) | New Relic |

| Unified observability and security solution<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Sumo Logic offers scalable log analytics, observability, SIEM and SOAR from one platform, helping DevSecOps and SRE teams get real-time insights to uncover and troubleshoot issues quickly.<br>New Relicâs strength is application performance monitoring (APM); they lack integrations with security vendors and donât support security use cases. |  |  |
| Full-stack observability powered by logs<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Sumo Logic and New Relic both address performance metrics, events and distributed transaction tracing. But no company matches Sumo Logic's ability to manage and analyze logs at scale.<br>Unlike New Relic, Sumo Logic centralizes log collection and applies machine learning to identify issues quickly, using analytics schema to address unparsed logs. |  |  |
| Advanced troubleshooting across all telemetry<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Powerful and flexible Sumo Logic Search Query Language allows searches across structured and unstructured data from metrics and traces to logs to deliver a better customer experience.<br>New Relic requires all log data to be pre-parsed to derive intelligence, with limited out-of-the-box connectors â and no pre-built dashboards for visualization. |  |  |
| Resilient & fault-tolerant with global scale<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Sumo Logicâs cloud-native, multi-tenant, microservices architecture ensures its platform is resilient and fault-tolerant, with data residency in North America (United States and Canada), Europe (Ireland and Germany) and Asia (Australia, India and Japan).<br>New Relic only recently moved to the cloud, challenging its resiliency and uptime. Its data residency is limited to North America (United States) and Europe (Germany). |  |  |

Moreover, moving from their Standard Plan (limited to five full platform users) to a Pro or Enterprise Plan will significantly increase licensing costs. |  |  |
| Unlimited users<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Sumo Logic offers unlimited user licenses meaning organizations donât have to restrict access to their analytics platform.<br>New Relicâs per-user licensing is a disincentive for widespread adoption and restricts access, limits visibility and impedes collaboration. |  |  |

## FAQ

Why would someone with New Relic switch to Sumo Logic?

For organizations that want a single source of truth, Sumo Logic can reduce your investment in analytics tools and provide visibility across your entire stack. Sumo Logic is a cloud-native platform powered by logs for multiple use cases, including APM and observability and security applications that span security analytics, SIEM and SOAR. Our flexible licensing model helps customers like The Pokemon Company, SAP and Alaska Airlines ingest massive amounts of machine data to quickly derive insights cost-effectively â without limiting users or use cases.

New Relic is an APM-focused solution that cannot support unstructured data (all its data must be pre-parsed, limiting visibility); it only recently moved to the cloud causing ongoing uptime challenges; and does not support security use cases. Expensive user-based licensing limits widespread monitoring and use, impeding the collaboration required to build, run, secure and manage modern applications.

What services does Sumo Logic offer to deliver a smooth tool and data migration from other platforms?

While getting started with Sumo Logic is easy, migration requires careful planning. If you are considering a New Relic alternative, assess what data sources and content you need to migrate to meet the needs of your current processes and use cases. Sumo Logic offers migration through our Professional Services to help you plan, design, implement and enable your team during and after the transition to our analytics platform. Users can access all public in-person and video training levels from beginner to advanced to get the most out of the tool. Sumo Logic includes [training and certifications](https://www.sumologic.com/learn/training/) with all its customer accounts.

To learn about a customer who underwent a large-scale data migration and tool consolidation to Sumo Logic, check out this [case study on Acquia](https://www.sumologic.com/case-study/acquia/).

How can Sumo Logic help me manage data ingest costs?

Sumo Logic's innovative approach to managing data helps customers save money while still ingesting large amounts of data. While all data is valuable, not all data is equal. Some use cases require "high touch" data to monitor and analyze application performance continuously or frequently. Other use cases require less systematic data analysis, like mining your infrastructure for insights or providing periodic reports.

Sumo Logic's [_Data Tiers_](https://help.sumologic.com/docs/manage/partitions-data-tiers/data-tiers/) provide a comprehensive solution for all types of data that an organization has â low touch, high touch and everything in between, at an economical price.

Customers of all sizes save money on data ingest using Sumo Logic Data Tiers. Learn how [Infor saved one million dollars in one year](https://www.sumologic.com/case-study/infor/) by applying Sumo Logic Data Tiering across its observability and security practices.

Will Sumo Logic scale as my business grows?

Sumo Logic is a cloud-native, multi-tenant platform designed to scale as your data and business grow. Built on a foundation of log management and [log analytics](https://www.sumologic.com/solutions/log-analytics/), it supports broad use cases, including real user monitoring, application monitoring, security analytics and audit and compliance. Growing teams use it to address application performance issues, security breaches and major incidents. Enterprise-grade features like unlimited users, multi-org help and role-based access control (RBAC) support your business as it matures.

Our [multi-cloud solutions](https://www.sumologic.com/multi-cloud/), including Amazon Web Services, Google Cloud Platform and Microsoft Azure, improve cloud infrastructure reliability and simplify and automate data collection. Global presence and data residency help businesses meet [data compliance](https://www.sumologic.com/solutions/audit-compliance/) and certification requirements wherever they are located.

Learn how we helped [Ulta Beauty](https://www.sumologic.com/case-study/ulta-beauty/) grow from a $200M business to a $2B e-commerce powerhouse.

How easy is it to get started with Sumo Logic?

Itâs super easy to [signup](https://www.sumologic.com/sign-up/) and get started. Register with your email for a free Sumo Logic account, including [Enterprise access](https://www.sumologic.com/pricing/) for the first thirty days. Start sending data to Sumo Logic and be up and running in minutes.

Or, use our [contact us](https://www.sumologic.com/contact-us/) form to speak with someone about migrating your data to Sumo Logic.

## Why is Sumo Logic a better alternative than Datadog?

Get full visibility into your applications and infrastructure without
sacrificing fidelity due to sampling, data silos, or overages with our
unified observability and security platform.

| [Download detailed comparison table](https://www.sumologic.com/brief/sumo-logic-delivers-greater-visibility-than-datadog/) | Sumo Logic | Datadog |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Application performance monitoring |  |  |
| Dynamic scalability |  |  |
| Advanced troubleshooting across all telemetry |  |  |
| Log search (query language) |  |  |
| APM/tracing and span analytics |  |  |
| Advanced security<br>(Security analytics + SIEM + SOAR) |  |  |
| Flexible licensing<br>No cost overages. No hidden costs. |  |  |
| Global presence and data residency |  |  |
| Free training and support |  |  |

### Make app reliability and security a team sport

Unified Application Observability

#### Sumo Logicâs full-stack observability suite provides:

- **Adaptive analytics**

Analytics on all structured and unstructured application data including transaction traces, logs and metrics.
- **Powerful query language and user-friendly UX**

Explore all data and find the unknown unknowns using pattern detection with AI/ML.
- **Open source collection**

Works with OpenTelemetry, Telegraf, and other open source tools.

![Service to infra temp](https://assets-www.sumologic.com/landing-pages/Service-to-infra-temp.jpg)

Simple and transparent licensing

#### Sumo Logicâs licensing model differs from Datadog:

- **Price transparency**

Eliminates license waste and on-demand overage bills.
- **Simplicity**

Single licensing model â no need to license every product or functionality.
- **Flexible data tiering**

Cost-effectively index all your data without sacrificing performance on our secure and compliant platform.

Most comprehensive security portfolio

#### Listed as a visionary in the SIEM Gartner Magic Quadrant, Sumo Logic supports the entire spectrum of security use cases:

- **Cloud Infrastructure Security**

Out-of-the-box apps and integrations for security and compliance content, for both cloud and on-premise data sources.
- **Cloud SIEM**

Automatically triage alerts and correlate threats across your entire environment.
- **Cloud SOAR**

Take your security to the next level with security orchestration, automation and response.

# The difference? We are cloud native. Splunk is not.

SUMO LOGIC VS SPLUNK

Get one unified cloud-native solution for all of your security and observability needs, and scale with ease.

- **Powerful Log Search**



Search anything, from logs to metrics, with Sumo Logic's easy-to-use query language. No sampling, just full-fidelity insights.

- **Flexible licensing**



Sumo Logic's pricing is easy on the wallet and adjusts to fit your data needs.

- **Advanced SIEM & SOAR**



Sumo Logic puts monitoring, security, and analytics all in one place.

## Why is Sumo Logic a better alternative than Splunk?

Splunk was built for silos not teams. See why it's time to get DevSecOps together and think logically.

| [Expand all](https://www.sumologic.com/compare/sumo-logic-vs-splunk/#) | ![Sumo Logic](https://www.sumologic.com/img/logo-black.svg) | Splunk |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Unified cloud-native platform<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Get real-time insights from Sumo Logicâs single, unified cloud-native platform across all your DevOps and SecOps use cases.<br>Splunk consists of legacy and multiple (5+) siloed products for observability and security, escalating the cost and complexity of Splunk deployments. |  |  |
| Dynamic scalability<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>There are no scalability limits on the Sumo Logic multi-tenant platform. It instantly scales each component of the architecture up or down to meet customer demand.<br>Splunk Cloud is a single-tenant lift-and-shift version of its on-prem Enterprise solution, requiring additional provisioning at additional cost for ingesting and searching at scale, including real-time search. |  |  |
| Robust, out-of-the-box security<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Sumo Logicâs compliance-ready solution comes standard with key attestations and security features, such as encryption-at-rest at no additional cost. | SOC 2 Type 2, PCI DSS 3.2, Privacy Shield, CSA Star & HIPAA certifications, FedRAMPÂ® Moderate Authorized, ISO 27001 | Pay more for encryption-at-rest (keys only rotate every six months), PCC and HIPAA-certified cloud environments. |
| Easy to set up and use<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Sumo Logic increases time-to-value by allowing customers to add users, data and third-party integrations themselves with an intuitive UIâno tickets required. <br>Splunkâs complex setup requires users to open a support ticket for basic configurations like installing specific apps, enabling real-time search & making administrative changes. |  |  |
| Free training and support<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>All beginner and advanced training and certification for observability and security solutions are free. Comprehensive enterprise support is available for all users. <br>With Splunk, you need to pay for all training and certification modules. |  |  |
| Flexible, cost-efficient pricing<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Sumo Logic's cost effect but high-performing data tiering, helps ensure cost control, and supports 30% more data than models based on daily peaks.<br>Splunkâs compute resource-based licensing significantly handicaps customers. Under provision and you run into significant performance problems in terms of concurrent searches and users. Because Splunk requires multiple products the overall price adds up quickly. |  |  |

## Your Choices Regarding Cookies on this Site

We use cookies and similar tracking technologies, and we allow our advertising partners to use such technologies, so we can, among other things, show you ads promoting Sumo Logic on other sites and services. These activities may be considered âsales,â âsharing,â or âtargeted advertisingâ under certain privacy laws, and you may have the right to opt out.
To opt-out of these activities, uncheck "All cookies" below. Note that you will need to renew this opt-out choice if you visit our website from another device or browser or if you clear your cookies. You can also opt out by visiting our website with a legally-recognized opt-out preference signal, such as the Global Privacy Control.

Allow All

### Manage Consent Preferences

#### Strictly Necessary Cookies

Always Active

These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

#### All cookies

All cookies

- ##### Performance Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.


- ##### Functional Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.


- ##### Targeting Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.

To enable organizations and teams to collaborate and resolve the hardest questions facing digital companies, powered by data-driven, actionable insights.

### Our purpose

Bring teams together to solve observability and security issues for digital companies.

## Your Choices Regarding Cookies on this Site

We use cookies and similar tracking technologies, and we allow our advertising partners to use such technologies, so we can, among other things, show you ads promoting Sumo Logic on other sites and services. These activities may be considered âsales,â âsharing,â or âtargeted advertisingâ under certain privacy laws, and you may have the right to opt out.
To opt-out of these activities, uncheck "All cookies" below. Note that you will need to renew this opt-out choice if you visit our website from another device or browser or if you clear your cookies. You can also opt out by visiting our website with a legally-recognized opt-out preference signal, such as the Global Privacy Control.

Allow All

### Manage Consent Preferences

#### Strictly Necessary Cookies

Always Active

These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

#### All cookies

All cookies

- ##### Performance Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.


- ##### Functional Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.


- ##### Targeting Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.

## Sumo Logic Leadership
[iframe](https://117583536.intellimizeio.com/storage.html)Our Leadership Team \| Sumo Logic

# Our leadership team

Sumo Logic unifies and analyzes enterprise data, translating it into actionable insights through its AI-powered cloud-native log analytics platform. This single source of truth enables Dev, Sec and Ops teams to simplify complexity, collaborate efficiently and accelerate data-driven decisions that drive business value.

## Your Choices Regarding Cookies on this Site

We use cookies and similar tracking technologies, and we allow our advertising partners to use such technologies, so we can, among other things, show you ads promoting Sumo Logic on other sites and services. These activities may be considered âsales,â âsharing,â or âtargeted advertisingâ under certain privacy laws, and you may have the right to opt out.
To opt-out of these activities, uncheck "All cookies" below. Note that you will need to renew this opt-out choice if you visit our website from another device or browser or if you clear your cookies. You can also opt out by visiting our website with a legally-recognized opt-out preference signal, such as the Global Privacy Control.

Allow All

### Manage Consent Preferences

#### Strictly Necessary Cookies

Always Active

These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

#### All cookies

All cookies

- ##### Performance Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.


- ##### Functional Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.


- ##### Targeting Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.

## Your Choices Regarding Cookies on this Site

We use cookies and similar tracking technologies, and we allow our advertising partners to use such technologies, so we can, among other things, show you ads promoting Sumo Logic on other sites and services. These activities may be considered âsales,â âsharing,â or âtargeted advertisingâ under certain privacy laws, and you may have the right to opt out.
To opt-out of these activities, uncheck "All cookies" below. Note that you will need to renew this opt-out choice if you visit our website from another device or browser or if you clear your cookies. You can also opt out by visiting our website with a legally-recognized opt-out preference signal, such as the Global Privacy Control.

Allow All

### Manage Consent Preferences

#### Strictly Necessary Cookies

Always Active

These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

#### All cookies

All cookies

- ##### Performance Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.


- ##### Functional Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.


- ##### Targeting Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.

## Sumo Logic vs Splunk
# The difference? We are cloud native. Splunk is not.

SUMO LOGIC VS SPLUNK

Get one unified cloud-native solution for all of your security and observability needs, and scale with ease.

- **Powerful Log Search**



Search anything, from logs to metrics, with Sumo Logic's easy-to-use query language. No sampling, just full-fidelity insights.

- **Flexible licensing**



Sumo Logic's pricing is easy on the wallet and adjusts to fit your data needs.

- **Advanced SIEM & SOAR**



Sumo Logic puts monitoring, security, and analytics all in one place.

## Why is Sumo Logic a better alternative than Splunk?

Splunk was built for silos not teams. See why it's time to get DevSecOps together and think logically.

| [Expand all](https://www.sumologic.com/compare/sumo-logic-vs-splunk/#) | ![Sumo Logic](https://www.sumologic.com/img/logo-black.svg) | Splunk |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Unified cloud-native platform<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Get real-time insights from Sumo Logicâs single, unified cloud-native platform across all your DevOps and SecOps use cases.<br>Splunk consists of legacy and multiple (5+) siloed products for observability and security, escalating the cost and complexity of Splunk deployments. |  |  |
| Dynamic scalability<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>There are no scalability limits on the Sumo Logic multi-tenant platform. It instantly scales each component of the architecture up or down to meet customer demand.<br>Splunk Cloud is a single-tenant lift-and-shift version of its on-prem Enterprise solution, requiring additional provisioning at additional cost for ingesting and searching at scale, including real-time search. |  |  |
| Robust, out-of-the-box security<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Sumo Logicâs compliance-ready solution comes standard with key attestations and security features, such as encryption-at-rest at no additional cost. | SOC 2 Type 2, PCI DSS 3.2, Privacy Shield, CSA Star & HIPAA certifications, FedRAMPÂ® Moderate Authorized, ISO 27001 | Pay more for encryption-at-rest (keys only rotate every six months), PCC and HIPAA-certified cloud environments. |
| Easy to set up and use<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Sumo Logic increases time-to-value by allowing customers to add users, data and third-party integrations themselves with an intuitive UIâno tickets required. <br>Splunkâs complex setup requires users to open a support ticket for basic configurations like installing specific apps, enabling real-time search & making administrative changes. |  |  |
| Free training and support<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>All beginner and advanced training and certification for observability and security solutions are free. Comprehensive enterprise support is available for all users. <br>With Splunk, you need to pay for all training and certification modules. |  |  |
| Flexible, cost-efficient pricing<br> <br>Show details<br> <br>Sumo Logic's cost effect but high-performing data tiering, helps ensure cost control, and supports 30% more data than models based on daily peaks.<br>Splunkâs compute resource-based licensing significantly handicaps customers. Under provision and you run into significant performance problems in terms of concurrent searches and users. Because Splunk requires multiple products the overall price adds up quickly. |  |  |

# Smooth sailing with Sumo Logic

Not sure how to navigate Kubernetes? Monitor, troubleshoot and secure your Kubernetes clusters with Sumo Logic Continuous Intelligence solution for Kubernetes. We'll show you the ropes, help you steer clear of risks, and spot problems before they start.

[Live demo](https://www.sumologic.com/events/kubernetes-live-demo/?utm_campaign=FY21Wayfinder&utm_term=live_demo)
Watch video


## Consider yourself unsinkable

From a hole in the hull to a storm headed your way, we've got you covered. As your environment changes so do the Sumo Logic dashboards reflecting the live state of your Kubernetes environment. See every pod in your Kubernetes environment and visually navigate from cluster to namespace, to service, pod, and container as you drill down and contain any leaks.

[Get eBook](https://www.sumologic.com/brief/kubernetes-observability/?utm_campaign=FY21Wayfinder&utm_term=kubernetes_observability_ebook)

## See more than meets the eye

Get a clear view of what's actually happening within your system. Our Continuous Intelligence Solution for Kubernetes lets you see the data through different lenses, giving you the ability to change perspectives. ## Save time and treasure

With Sumo Logic, security comes standard. Our out-of-the-box integration with Falco enables you to see security threats in context right alongside your logs and metrics. Take security even further with Sumo Logic's Cloud SIEM functionality for a top to bottom DevSecOps viewâfrom your Kubernetes clusters, to your application, to cloud and on-premise infrastructure.

[Watch webinar](https://www.sumologic.com/webinar/kubernetes-phenomenon/?utm_campaign=FY21Wayfinder&utm_term=kubernetes_webinar)

## Get up and runningâfast

Set up data collection in no time. We've got it all preconfigured, so you can streamline your collection process to filter just the data you need. With a single helm install command, you'll configure an entire cluster to collect logs, metrics, events, and security data. With your data streaming into Sumo Logic, pre-built dashboards give you top to bottom visibility of your environment, and even stay up to date as pods are added or removed.

## Your Choices Regarding Cookies on this Site

We use cookies and similar tracking technologies, and we allow our advertising partners to use such technologies, so we can, among other things, show you ads promoting Sumo Logic on other sites and services. These activities may be considered âsales,â âsharing,â or âtargeted advertisingâ under certain privacy laws, and you may have the right to opt out.
To opt-out of these activities, uncheck "All cookies" below. Note that you will need to renew this opt-out choice if you visit our website from another device or browser or if you clear your cookies. You can also opt out by visiting our website with a legally-recognized opt-out preference signal, such as the Global Privacy Control.

Allow All

### Manage Consent Preferences

#### Strictly Necessary Cookies

Always Active

These cookies are necessary for the website to function and cannot be switched off in our systems. They are usually only set in response to actions made by you which amount to a request for services, such as setting your privacy preferences, logging in or filling in forms. You can set your browser to block or alert you about these cookies, but some parts of the site will not then work. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable information.

#### All cookies

All cookies

- ##### Performance Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies allow us to count visits and traffic sources so we can measure and improve the performance of our site. They help us to know which pages are the most and least popular and see how visitors move around the site. All information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous. If you do not allow these cookies we will not know when you have visited our site, and will not be able to monitor its performance.


- ##### Functional Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies enable the website to provide enhanced functionality and personalisation. They may be set by us or by third party providers whose services we have added to our pages. If you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly.


- ##### Targeting Cookies




Switch Labellabel



These cookies may be set through our site by our advertising partners. They may be used by those companies to build a profile of your interests and show you relevant adverts on other sites. They do not store directly personal information, but are based on uniquely identifying your browser and internet device. If you do not allow these cookies, you will experience less targeted advertising.
